class=\"content-ad-block navigation-not-searchable\"><div id=\"rocketleague_336x280_BTF\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"fo-nttax-infobox-wrapper\"><div class=\"fo-nttax-infobox wiki-bordercolor-light\"><div><div class=\"infobox-header wiki-backgroundcolor-light\">Upcoming Matches</div></div></div></div>\n<p><b>RLCS 2021-22 </b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2021, crossing over into 2022. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with more regions and an updated format. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each have 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collects points that will determine whether they will qualify for the World Championship or World Championship Wildcard.\n</p><p>The <b>RLCS 2021-22 Winter Split Major</b> took place in Los Angeles, United States at the <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https://www.faceit.com/en\">FACEIT Studio</a> and the <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https://www.youtubetheater.com/\">YouTube Theater</a>.\n</p>\n<div id=\"toc\" class=\"toc\" role=\"navigation\" href=\"#Streams\">Streams</a> section.</small></li></ul>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Format\">Format</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/2021-22/Winter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14\" title=\"Edit section: Format\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>March 23rd - 25th, 2022</i>\n<ul><li>16 teams - split into 4 groups of 4.</li>\n<li>Round Robin <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr>\n<ul><li>Tiebreakers:\n<ul><li>In the event of 2 teams being tied on the same record, a <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr> tiebreaker match will be played out to separate the two teams.</li>\n<li>In the event of 3 teams being tied on the same record, the following 3 tiebreakers will be used with the order outlined below to remove one of the teams from the contention towards a tiebreaker match:\n<ul><li>Game Differential</li>\n<li>Game Differential among tied teams</li>\n<li>Initial Seed</li></ul></li>\n<li>When 3 teams tie on a 2-1 record, the team that places lowest within the tiebreaker criteria will be awarded 3rd place in the group. The other 2 teams will play a <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr> tiebreaker match for 1st place.</li>\n<li>When 3 teams tie on a 1-2 record, the team that places highest within the tiebreaker criteria will be awarded 2nd place in the group. The other 2 teams will play a <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr> tiebreaker match for 3rd place.</li></ul></li></ul></li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(232,221,239);\">Winner</span> of each group qualifies to the Winners' Bracket of the <a href=\"#Playoffs\">Playoffs</a>.</li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(221,244,221);\">Places 2 and 3</span> of each group qualify to the Losers' Bracket of the <a href=\"#Playoffs\">Playoffs</a>.</li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(251,223,223);\">4th place</span> of each group is eliminated.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<p><br />\n</p>\n<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>March 25th - 27th, 2022</i> - <i>Crowd Days: March 26th &amp; 27th</i>\n<ul><li>Double Elimination Bracket.\n<ul><li>Upper Bracket: All matches are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr>.</li>\n<li>Lower Bracket: Round 1 and 2 are <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr>. Quarterfinals, Semifinals and Finals are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr>.</li>\n<li>Grand Finals are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> with a Bracket Reset, where the team coming from the Lower Finals must win 2 <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> series.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Prize_Pool\">Prize Pool</span><span title=\"Edit section: Prize Pool\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>$300,000 <abbr title=\"United States Dollar\">USD</abbr> and <a
